 bharat or bangladesh ke bich june main hua jameen kii adla-badali kaa aitihaasik samjhauta 1 agast se lagu ho rahaa he
 With the implementation of this agreement, 111 colonies of India will become Bangladesh and 51 colonies of Bangladesh will be of India
 bharat main jin rajyon kii coloniyon kii adla-badali hogi, vah hai assam, meghalaya, tripura or pashchimbengal
 According to an estimate, about 37 thousand people live in the Indian colonies under this decision
 vahiin bangladeshi coloniyaan main 14 hajaar log rahete hai
 That is, these new 14 thousand citizens of the country will get the gift of new PIN code today
 bharat kii coloniyon main rahane vaale kareeb 37 hazaar logon main se 980 log hi bharat laut rahe hai or ye sabhi behad garib tabake hai
 The deal was signed between India and Bangladesh during Prime Minister Narendra Modi's first visit to Bangladesh in June
 is daure kii khaas baat yah bhi thi ki pashchim bengal kii siem mamata banerjee bhi pradhanmantri ke saath bangladesh gai thim jabaki purv pradhanmantri manmohan singh ke bangladesh daure ke vakt unhone jane se inkaar kar diya tha
 Prime Minister Narendra Modi compared this agreement to the fall of the Berlin Wall, saying that if such an agreement had been done elsewhere in the world, it would have received Nobel Honor, but we are poor country so no one would ask
 bharat or bangladesh ke is samjhaute ke chalate jahaan bangladesh ko 10 hajaar acre jameen milegi, vahiin bharat ko sirf 500 acre jameen milegi
 The agreement was passed by the Parliament in India in May
 iskaa zikr karte hue pradhanmantri modi ne bangladesh main kaha tha ki bharat kii sasand main sabhi dalon ke dwaara paarit kiye gaye is samjhaute se pataa chalata he ki bangladesh or bharat kitne ahm sahyogi hai
 The comments bharat or bangladesh ke bich zamin kii adla-badali kaa pehla samjhauta 16 may 1974 ko tatkaaleen pradhanmantri indira gandhi or bangladesh ke pradhanmantri mujiburr rahamaan ke bich hua tha
 The parliament of Bangladesh approved the agreement in 1974, but the exchange of land for the agreement required a constitutional amendment in India, which took so long to finalize the agreement
 isi samjhaute ke lagu hone ke saath bharat kii 111 coloniyaan bangladesh kii ho jaaengi or or bangladesh kii 51 coloniyaan bharat kii

 pradhanmantri narendra modi ne is samjhaute kii tulana berlin kii diwaar girane vaali ghatana se karte hue kaha tha ki agar is tarah kaa samjhauta duniya main kahin or hua hota to ise nobel sammaan miltaa, lekin ham garib desh hai isliye koi nahin poochhega
 Due to this agreement between India and Bangladesh, while Bangladesh will get 10,000 acres of land, India will get only 500 acres
 is samjhaute ko bharat main may maheene main sansad ne paas kiya tha

 kuch hi dinon pehle apni beti ko kho dene vaali mashhoor gayika aashaa bhonsle ne kaha, jab main apni beti ko kho dene ke gam se ubar hi rahi hum mere bhai yash chopra bhaisaab mujhe chhodkar chale gaye hai
 Famous actor Dilip Kumar, who played the lead role in Chopra's 1984 film 'mashal', tweeted, 'shocking, hard to believe
 yash ek dost or bhai se kahin badhkar the
 i am shocked and i have no words to express my grief
 swar kokila lata mangeshkar ne unhen hansmukh evam sahruday vyaktitv vaale ek bhai ke taur par yaad kiya
 Lata wrote, Yash Chopra was like my brother
 unke film-nirmaan kaa tarika kaaphi alag tha or sangeet ke najariye se bhi unki filmein hit hoti thim
 The magic of his films' music never faded
 hansmukh evam sahruday vyaktitv tha unka
 i last spoke to him on his birthday and after that he became ill
 maine sochaa ki vah thik ho jaaenge
 Madhuri Dixit wrote, just got the news that Yashji is no more
 vah cinema ke diggajon main se ek the
 My deepest condolences to his family
 hamen unki kami hameshaa khalegi
 The comments 'vir jaaraa’ film main chopra ke saath kaam kar chukin adaakara priti jinta ne ‘twit’ kiya, yash ankal hamen aapaki kami hameshaa mahasoos hogi
 May your soul rest in peace
 filmkaar mahesh bhatta ne kaha, aazaadee ke baad bhartiya cinema main yash chopra kaa yogadan ahm rahaa he
 In his last film Jab Tak Hai Jaan, he gave his everything
 vah kaaphi sakriy vyakti the
 Shabana Azmi said, Yashji, how can you go? On your 80th birthday we wished you to make 80 more films
 
 It is heartbreaking
 abhinayta akshay kumaar ne kaha, main sadame main hum or stabdh hum, khabar par yakeen nahin kar saktaa, pyaar ko amar kar dene vaale shaks chopra nahin rahe bhagwaan unki aatma ko shanti de
 My deepest condolences to the family
 mahanayake amitabh bachchan ne ‘twit’ kiya, ‘‘yash chopra nahin rahe
 
 ab se takreeban ek ghanta pehle
 Actress Sridevi, who worked in 'chandni' and 'lamhe' alongside Chopra, tweeted, 'I am deeply saddened by the news of Yashji's death
